Kita selesaikan terlebih dahulu SPLTV yang kita\nperoleh di atas.<br \/>\n2x + y + z = 11.000\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 (1)<br \/>\nx + 3y + 2z = 16.500\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 (2)<br \/><\/span>2x + 2y + z = 13.000\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 <span>(3)<br \/>\nEliminasi x dan z dari (1) dan (2).<br \/>\n2x + y + z = 11.000<\/span><br \/>\n2x + 2y + z = 13.000<br \/><span>--------------------------- \u00a0-<br \/>\n\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 - y\u00a0 =\u00a0\n-2.000<br \/><\/span>\u2194<span>\u00a0 y = 2.000\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 (4)<br \/>\nSubstitusikan (4) ke (2), diperoleh:<br \/>\nx + 3(2.000) + 2z = 16.500<br \/><\/span>\u2194<span> x + 6.000 + 2z = 16.500<br \/><\/span><span>\u2194 x = 16.500 \u2013 6.000 \u2013 2z<br \/>\n\u2194 x = 10.500 \u2013 2z\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0\u00a0 (5) <br \/>\nSubstitusikan (4) dan (5) ke (1).<br \/>\n2(10.500 \u2013 2z) + 2.000 + z = 11.000<br \/>\n\u2194 21.000 \u2013 4z + 2.000 + z = 11.000<br \/>\n\u2194 -3z = 11.000 \u2013 21.000 \u2013 2.000<br \/>\n\u2194 -3z = -12.000<br \/>\n\u2194 z = 4.000<br \/>\nSubstitusikan nilai z = 4.000 ke (5).<br \/>\nx = 10.500 \u2013 2z = 10.500 \u2013 2(4.000) = 10.500 \u2013 8.000 = 2.500<br \/>\nKita peroleh:<br \/><\/span><span>harga penghapus = x =\n2.500 <br \/>\nharga rautan = y = 2.000<br \/>\nharga penggaris = z = 4.000<br \/>\nJadi, untuk 2 penghapus, 3 rautan, dan 1 penggaris, Rita harus membayar:<br \/>\n2(2.500) + 3(2.000) + 4.000 = 5.000 + 6.000 + 4.000 = 15.000 rupiah.<\/span><\/p>",
